90,000 People Hold Anti-Government Rally in London 58

MacDonald's Declaration Maintains Status Quo

Time Not Yet Ripe to Restore Party System

London – This afternoon, approximately 90,000 people gathered in Trafalgar Square to listen to speeches by about 30 representatives from political parties, industry, religious, educational, and peace societies, who vehemently criticized the government's anti-sedition bill. Five hundred police officers, mostly mounted, were present to maintain order, but the crowd was generally well-behaved. The crowd then passed a resolution denouncing the government's bill as a major impediment to the traditional liberties of Great Britain and demanded its withdrawal. Left-wing Labour MP McGovern gave a passionate speech, extensively discussing the section in Philip Gibbs' war memoir that criticized General Haig, the commander-in-chief of the British Army during the European War, for wasting British soldiers' lives in Flanders, Belgium. His words were so intense that they moved the audience. (Reuters, 28th)

London – Recently, the government proposed a bill requesting Parliament to allow the government to punish propaganda campaigns of a disruptive nature that could undermine the loyalty of the army to the Crown. The opposition Labour Party believes this bill is aimed at suppressing populist unrest and has launched a campaign among people from all walks of life to express their opposition. They posted slogans in Trafalgar Square, boldly stating, "Our freedom or your laws, one cannot exist with the other." Over four thousand people gathered in the square, cheering and demonstrating. The British people's concern for political freedom is evident here. Labour Party members also humorously pointed out that if the government's bill had been passed before the European War, the literary giant George Bernard Shaw and Prime Minister MacDonald himself would have been arrested long ago and spent the four years of the war in prison. Prime Minister MacDonald will attend a banquet of the National Labour Committee tomorrow and deliver a speech, a large part of which will be used to discuss this issue. Its great importance can be imagined. (Havas, 28th)

London – The National Labour Party entertained Prime Minister MacDonald today. Many important government officials were present. MacDonald delivered a speech in which he said that a government of national unity has created trust and security and should therefore be maintained. The country is not yet ready to return to party politics. He appealed to the British people, especially the youth, to view the government of national unity as a manifestation of a great philosophy of social progress. Security and organized evolution are a policy that can advance the country without being subject to disruptive interruptions of continuity, which is the opposite of harsh measures and revolution. Lord President of the Council Baldwin then spoke, saying that there was no sign of a return to a major party succession in the near future. (Reuters, 29th)

British Parliament Opens Today 59

London – The British Parliament is scheduled to reopen tomorrow to discuss a great many matters. The session is expected to last until late at night. The legislative bills to be handled include gambling and lottery cases and the sedition bill. It is expected that the opposition party will use these cases to attack the government. Questions to be raised by members of Parliament at tomorrow's meeting will include the European situation, disarmament, war debts, the report of the Joint Committee on Indian Constitutional Reform, and issues such as assistance to the British shipping industry. It is expected that the current session will end on November 16th. A new session will begin four days later. (Reuters, 29th)

The Soviet Russian government has recently issued serious warnings to officials in all departments and has begun to crack down on all major and minor cases of fraud. Molotov on Current Issues in the Soviet Union 61

Moscow – Molotov, Chairman of the Council of People's Commissars of the Soviet Union, wrote an article on the Soviet elections, saying, "We can be justly proud of the achievements of the Soviet regime. Today, only we have opened up a path of cultural development for the Soviet people. Our great task today is to fully utilize all our production resources, build new factories, power plants, and mines, etc. These undertakings are all beneficial to our motherland. We have, as required by reality, undergone a period of training and overcoming new technologies. This is especially true in the countryside. Only if we more fully utilize the shameful idleness of all the machinery in collective and state-owned farms, can the harvests of grains, sugar beets, flax, and cotton be rapidly increased. Our country has many economic possibilities that have not yet been utilized. Our development is quite impressive. All that we need is to strive for the utilization of new enterprises and new technologies, and at the same time, to achieve this, we must intensify the improvement of the cultural level of the masses, increase labor discipline, and increase the responsibility of leaders for their work. The Communist Party demands an intensified struggle against the bureaucracy of the entire national administration. A concrete and effective leadership, combined with supervision and execution, has become the slogan of the Communist Party in the practical work of all departments. The Communist Party strictly requires personnel serving the national economy to deeply study the technology of the positions they hold, overcome production methods, and truly take on the responsibilities they bear.

Our country's non-Party intellectuals are also developing. The growth of such personnel, both within and outside the Party, especially the growth of Soviet youth, is a guarantee of our future success. The scale of this success should not be underestimated. The system adopted in our country is indeed laying a solid foundation for the growing development of these new forces. At present, the need for culture is most enormous. This is why our country urgently needs culture. They strive for culture and strive to satisfy their demands. At the same time, this is why the Soviet regime was created by the working masses of our country. These issues, at the time of these Soviet re-elections, will be expressed with new strength to hundreds of millions of toiling masses, and at the same time will have greater significance for the work of the newly elected Soviets.

We believe that at the time of re-elections, any person who is hostile to the Soviet regime will never dare to openly show their face. However, this must not lead us to consider the resistance to all anti-Soviet actions of our class enemies, the exposure of all unreliable elements entering the Soviets, and the abandonment of all opportunistic and liberal rhetoric as unnecessary. The Soviets we need are the battle organizations for the working masses to fight against their class enemies. Our enemies will eventually understand the invincible enthusiasm of millions of socialist builders, or they will disarm or cease their anti-Soviet actions and their opposition to the collective farming system, or they will inevitably suffer the merciless blow of the proletariat dictatorship, which is dedicated to self-defense.

The international position of the Soviet Republic, especially its position as a factor for general peace, is increasing day by day. This is a well-known fact. The Soviet Union's position as a strong country capable of destroying imperialist aggression has even made the bourgeoisie look up with respect and view the Soviet Union as a world power." (TASS, 28th)

Japan Considers Tax Increase 63

Tokyo – Finance Minister Fujii has now established a special wartime profits tax, which is expected to increase tax revenue by up to 100 million yen. He also plans to increase revenue through other methods. It is reported that an increase in postal rates may increase revenue by approximately 30 million yen, and an increase in the railway profits account may increase revenue in the general account by approximately 30 million yen. Adding these two items to the increase in the wartime profits tax, the total amount is expected to reach 100 million yen. The Finance Minister plans to discuss all the above points with former Finance Minister Takahashi and seek his understanding. (Japan United Press, 29th)

Tokyo – At 3:50 p.m. this afternoon, Prime Minister Okada visited former Finance Minister Takahashi at his private residence in Akasaka to exchange views on the tax increase issue. He left at 5:10 p.m. After the meeting, former Finance Minister Takahashi said that Prime Minister Okada's visit was aimed at seeking my opinion on the succession of the budget for the next fiscal year. The contents cannot be disclosed. As for the preparation of the budget, Finance Minister Fujii is working hard on it, so I have nothing more to say at this time. However, the tax increase issue was indeed discussed. (Denstu, 29th)

Tokyo – When the government prepares the budget for the next fiscal year, whether or not to implement a tax increase has attracted the attention of the financial community and all sectors. Finance Minister Fujii, in view of the political, economic, and social circumstances, decided to increase tax revenue. Therefore, on the 27th, he visited former Finance Minister Takahashi for an hour and a half, expressed his views on the tax increase, and requested his understanding. After considering the measures in the past two or three days, Finance Minister Fujii met with Prime Minister Okada, obtained his consent, and formally decided on the tax increase policy.

The extent of Finance Minister Fujii's tax increase plan is approximately 30 million or 100 million yen. The industries that will be affected by the tax increase are export industries, military industries, industries, the securities industry, and the construction industry. Finance Minister Fujii plans to increase the special income tax, not the general customs duties.

The contents of Finance Minister Fujii's tax increase plan are as follows:

1. Compare the income determination amount for Showa 9 (1934) with the income determination amount for Showa 5 (1930) and Showa 6 (1931). The average increase will be determined as special income.

2. The tax rate is set at 10% proportional tax, but the loss calculation at the time of gold export prohibition and the newly established ones are set at 8%.

3. The implementation period is tentatively set for three or five years. (Japan United Press, 29th)

Tokyo – Although Finance Minister Fujii has decided to implement the tax increase, Prime Minister Okada had previously stated that there would be no tax increase in the next fiscal year, so he does not approve of the tax increase plan. Moreover, except for the Minister of the Army, other cabinet members have considerable disagreements regarding the tax increase. Therefore, Finance Minister Fujii's proposed tax increase plan will inevitably encounter considerable turmoil until the two houses make a decision. (Denstu, 29th)

Siam Troubled: Finance and Military are the Key Issues 64

Situation Worsens After Revolution

Rumor That the King of Siam Will Never Return Home Has Been Around for a Long Time

London – Siamese bonds were weak today, but the general public in the stock exchange is now eagerly awaiting accurate news on the situation in Siam. A retired senior official who had lived in Siam for many years and still has close contact with the situation in Siam told a Reuters reporter today that although Siam appears peaceful on the surface and the Siamese people are peace-loving, the political circles are currently very turbulent. The fundamental difficulties at present are half due to finance and half due to the military. The revolution in 1932 made the military aware of the need to compete for power. This was the first time in Siamese history. Since then, the military's competition for power has become a disruptive factor. The government established after the revolution abolished miscellaneous taxes to win the hearts of the people. As a result, national income was greatly reduced, and the country often struggled financially. In addition, when the King and Queen of Siam traveled to Europe last time, they spent a large amount of money purchasing machinery, believing that this would benefit the development of Siamese industries. As a result, the finances became even more strained. The Minister of Finance exhausted all means to pay for this amount. When the King of Siam went to England this spring, rumors spread that the King would never return home. (Reuters, 29th)

Representatives Around the King of Siam Express 65

Striving for Privileges and Supporting Democratic Governance

No News of Incidents Occurring in the Country

London – Today, the King of Siam, through his private secretary, made a clear statement to a Reuters reporter that his struggle for the privilege of pronouncing the death penalty is actually a struggle to uphold the principles of democratic government. The elected members of parliament are now mostly opposed to the plan to strip the king of his powers. Therefore, his refusal to sign the new bill is directly based on the wishes of the majority of the people. He feels that the people do not want to change the current system. Therefore, the King of Siam's intention to abdicate has the nature of a démarche expressing grief to his government. The government can only completely abandon the new plan, submit it to a public vote, or hold a general election to avoid the King of Siam's abdication. So far, the King of Siam and the government have not directly negotiated. The King of Siam entrusted his regent in Bangkok with his intention to abdicate to the government about ten days ago. The government has strongly urged the King of Siam to reconsider his decision. Since announcing his intention to abdicate, the King of Siam has not received any news of incidents or revolutions occurring in the country. At present, only the Siamese government has asked the King to reconsider his decision. The Siamese military and other circles have not taken such action. (Reuters, 28th)

Issue of Establishing a Central Bank in the United States 74

Washington – Although the relationship between bankers and the government in Washington has greatly improved recently, financial leaders still believe that the government will control the banking industry. It has been learned from reliable sources today that the Treasury Department is still studying banking legislation to expand the Federal Reserve Board, so that the Federal Reserve Board will fully become a central bank. However, the Associated Press has learned that the Treasury Department's experts will not submit their investigation report to Treasury Secretary Morgenthau in the next seven weeks. Although President Roosevelt ridiculed the proposal to establish a central bank last week and repeatedly reaffirmed his confidence in the profit system and the use of private capital to finance industries, the idea of a central bank is still suspected by all sectors. Some people say that the funds lent by the central banker, the unified banking system, avoid conflicts in lending policies between banks, and organize a committee to be solely responsible for the central bank. Generally speaking, the central bank of the United States, no matter what form it takes, will make the government's control more obvious than the current Federal Reserve Board. Currently, 6,300 of the 15,500 banks nationwide belong to the Federal Reserve Board. Therefore, most bankers have recognized it as a central bank, because it not only determines the discount rate within the twelve Federal Reserve districts, but also promotes the government's financial reform policies in a timely manner. Another central bank function of the Federal Reserve Board is that the cash used by the Federal Reserve Board exceeds more than half of the national currency. The Federal Reserve Board also determines all banking and lending policies for the twelve Federal Reserve districts to adopt. (National Telegraph, 28th)

She Hanged Her Child on a Tree Branch

Beiping: Yesterday morning, an infant, barely over one year old, was discovered on a willow tree next to the Second Gate of the Dongbianmen outside the city. Japanese Newspaper Reports on Russian Border Security Against Manchukuo 86

Yesterday, the Shanghai Japanese newspaper reported that, according to recent intelligence, the Soviet Union's security measures along the border with Manchuria are extremely strict. Da Meng Da Zhi (each location has 10 Mongolian surveillance soldiers); 7. Bo Luo Nuo Er (36 Mongolian surveillance soldiers); 8. Ai Lun Si (10 surveillance soldiers). The Ai Lun Si observation post is located on the border line. The other observation posts were established based on terrain and water access. Security arrangements include one sentry on duty during the day, and two mounted patrols at night. Four patrol teams are organized for mutual communication. San Peng De Men has the 5th and 7th Regiments with 1,000 cavalry, six mountain guns, and two field guns; 3. Han Xiang De has 500 Mongolian soldiers; 4. National Army Recaptures Ningdu 87

Remnants of the Bandits Retreat Southwest Towards Yudu

Refugees From Weifeng Recall Their Resistance Against the Bandits

Nanchang Correspondence: Ningdu is a large county in southern Jiangxi with a dense population and fertile land. It is interwoven with Nanfeng, Le'an, and Yongfeng to the north. The terrain is complex and dangerous. Wangpo, Xiaopu, Kuzhu, and other notorious bandit lairs are scattered throughout the area. To the east, it is connected to Xingguo, Guangchang, and Shicheng. To the west, it adjoins Yongfeng, Xingguo, Yudu. To the south, it directly reaches Ruijin. Militarily, geographically, and economically, it is crucial to the Red bandits. The National Army’s First Route Army, after capturing the transportation hub of Guangchang, Shicheng and Ningdu, advanced on both sides, simultaneously capturing Shicheng and Ningdu. After the successive capture of Shicheng's Gulonggang and Ningdu, the momentum for annihilation was established. The false Third Army Corps retreated from Shicheng towards eastern Ningdu, and the false Eighth Army Corps and the false First Army Corps retreated from Xingguo Gulonggang to Qingtang (the border between Ningdu and Yudu). Although they wanted to defend their positions to the death, the firepower of the National Army’s airplanes and cannons was overwhelming. They fled southwest towards Yudu and Huichang. The National Army, in order to quickly complete the task of eradicating the bandits, launched a joint attack on Ningdu for several days. The operation progressed extremely rapidly. The headquarters recently received a telephone call from the Northern Route Army headquarters, stating that Zhou’s division of Chen Cheng’s Third Route Army captured Ningdu County on the evening of the 26th. Refugees have entered the city to comfort the people, repair fortifications, and conduct post-war relief efforts, while continuing to advance on the bandits. According to records, the Red bandits, led by Zhu De and Mao Zedong, entered Ningdu several times in 1928. The National Army gained and lost the city in turns. In 1929, it was completely occupied by the bandits. In 1930, the Third Route Army launched a major campaign to suppress the bandits, and the city was recovered temporarily. Sun Lianzhong's division of the Twenty-sixth Route Army was stationed there. However, on December 15, 1931, Zhao Bosheng suddenly led Dong Zhentang and Ji Zhentong in a mutiny. They were incorporated into the Red bandit forces as the false Fifth Army Corps. Ningdu fell into the hands of the bandits once again. For several years since then, production facilities have been completely destroyed, and countless men and women have died. The entire county is scorched earth, a heartbreaking sight. Recovery will take decades of cultivation. However, since the rebel Zhao Bosheng reoccupied Ningdu in 1931, groups of refugees fled to mountain strongholds to resist the bandits. There were as many as dozens of these strongholds. These strongholds were like isolated islands in the sea to the bandits. They maintained their integrity and defended themselves for two years. When the strongholds fell, the entire population died as bravely as Tian Heng's followers, without a single surrender. Cuiwei Peak is one such example. The peak is located ten miles from the county seat and is a steep, towering peak. The summit covers hundreds of acres and was the place where sages of past generations studied and lectured. There are fields, ponds, wells, and thatched cottages. There is only a single hole carved between two rocks that can be climbed to ascend, with no other passages. Since the refugees defended it in December 1931, the bandits repeatedly besieged it, but failed to capture it. During that time, high-ranking military agencies sent planes to supply the refugees with salt and bullets. The refugees eventually reached the point of exchanging children for food, until the stronghold was finally broken by the bandits in January 1933. At that time, refugees jumped into wells, committed suicide, killed their children, or husbands killed their wives before killing themselves. The entire stronghold sacrificed itself, making it a heroic and tragic story in the resistance against the bandits. (October 27th)

Page 9

Japanese Actively Expanding the Southeast Asian Market 88

Dispatching Commercial Commissioners to Siam for Inspection

Annual Sales of Japanese Goods to Siam Exceed 10 Million Gold

Bangkok Special Correspondent: Since British Malaya and the Dutch East Indies have implemented trade controls and restricted the import of Japanese goods, the Japanese goods market in Southeast Asia has been severely impacted. Japanese merchants have panicked and demanded that their government negotiate with the colonial authorities of Britain and the Netherlands. However, the British government, in order to protect its major Lancashire textile market from being taken over, seems to be determined to restrict the import of Japanese cotton textiles into its Southeast Asian colonies. Therefore, although the Japanese have protested many times, they have been ineffective. As for the Dutch side, after the Dutch East Indies government announced import restrictions on 56 commodities, the Dutch-Japanese conference was convened to ease tensions due to the serious protests from the Japanese side. However, the conference has been going on for months since it opened in mid-June, with reports of progress and tension at times. So far, there has been no progress. Under such circumstances, the Japanese are unwilling to sit idly by and await their demise, and can only seek alternative routes in Southeast Asia to find outlets for their goods.

In addition to the colonies of Britain and the Netherlands, the other islands of Southeast Asia, such as the American-controlled Philippines and the French-controlled Annam, have high tariff barriers to prevent the large-scale import of goods from non-sovereign countries. Therefore, Japan cannot satisfy its desires in these two places either. As a result of agonizing and energetic efforts, the Japanese are planning to expand a new market. What is this new market? It is Siam. Siam is located on the Indochina Peninsula, northeast of the Malay Peninsula, and is the only independent country in Southeast Asia. It covers an area of approximately 195,000 square miles and has a population of approximately 10 million. The people are mainly engaged in agriculture. With the exception of rice mills and sawmills, other light and heavy industries are extremely backward, making it an excellent market for industrial products. In the past, Siam also had considerable political ties with Japan. For example, when the League of Nations voted last year to deny recognition of the puppet state of Manchukuo, representatives from countries around the world unanimously voted against it, while the Siamese representative abstained, expressing goodwill towards Japan. Therefore, now that Japan is facing restrictions on the import of its goods by various Southeast Asian colonies, it has no choice but to expand its market in Siam to seek remedy.

According to sources here, the Osaka Japanese Chamber of Commerce, on the pretext of improving the current state of trade between Japan and Siam, will soon send a commercial commissioner to Siam for negotiations. Its purpose is self-evident. In recent years, the annual import of Japanese goods into Siam has exceeded 12 million Japanese yen (approximately 8 million Siamese baht), while the annual import of Siamese products into Japan is only worth 800,000 Japanese yen (approximately 600,000 Siamese baht). Japan's trade surplus with Siam has exceeded 11 million Japanese yen, and it is still actively planning to expand. Although it is said that the restrictions imposed by Britain and the Netherlands are inevitable, Japan's ambition cannot be concealed. If we look back at the situation of our country's trade with Siam, the difference is incalculable. According to a survey, from January to August of this year, the total value of Siamese products imported into our country was 25.5 million yuan, while during the same period, our country's exports to Siam were only 8.8 million yuan. Our trade deficit reached more than 16.7 million yuan. Moreover, there are approximately 2.5 million overseas Chinese in Siam, dozens or hundreds of times more than the number of Japanese residents.

Inside Truths of the Jiangxi Bandits 89

Notes Published by Yang Yuebin,

Pseudo-Central Minister of Armed Forces, After Surrendering to the National Army

Xiamen Correspondence: Yang Yuebin, the Red Bandit’s Central Mobilization Minister of Armed Forces, who recently escaped from the bandit area of Ninghua and surrendered to the Third Division's Special Party Department in Liancheng, recently published notes recording the true situation inside the bandit areas. The following is an excerpt of the important parts:

Since the Fujian Incident and the failure of the 19th Route Army, the bandits have been severely impacted. After the Central Army's five encirclement and suppression campaigns and the successive capture of Guangchang, Jianning, and Liancheng, the bandits organized expanded Red Army assault teams and economic movement assault teams in the bandit areas, forcing men between the ages of 16 and 45 to join the Red Army, resulting in over 53,000 soldiers. They extorted over 200,000 piculs of grain. The pseudo-Central Military Commission attempted to concentrate all its forces in the area between Ruijin and Shicheng, or near Ruijin, for a final desperate gamble, preserving the military equipment accumulated by the Red bandits over the years and calling on other bandit areas to preserve the so-called Central Soviet Area. If the decisive battle failed, they would break up a part of their forces into smaller units, scattering them throughout Fujian and Jiangxi. The main force would be regrouped and flee through Anyuan, Xinfeng, and Sannan into southern Hunan, escaping to Sichuan or the Yunnan-Guizhou border to join forces with the Xu and He bandits, attempting to enter Sichuan. Between April and May, the pseudo-Central government had already transferred many cadres from the bandit army who were natives of southern Hunan, secretly returning them to various counties in southern Hunan to establish communication lines. The bandits in southern Jiangxi and western Fujian originally consisted of the 3rd, 4th, 5th, 7th, 12th, and 13th Armies, which were reorganized into the 1st, 3rd, and 5th Army Corps. The 10th Army was stationed in the northeast. Since August of last year, the bandit leader Peng Dehuai led the 5th and 7th Armies to occupy Yangkou. After the Russian Li De infiltrated the bandit area, he reorganized the bandit army, abolished the army system, and strengthened the combat troops, adding battalion headquarters. The division was established as a fixed organizational unit. The pseudo-Third Army was renamed the First Division, the pseudo-Seventh Army was renamed the Fifth Division, the pseudo-Thirteenth Army was renamed the Thirteenth Division, and the pseudo-Twelfth Army was renamed the Thirty-fourth Division. In addition, civilians were recruited in the bandit areas and reorganized into the Red Garrison Army and guerrilla teams, forming the Third, Sixth, Fourteenth, Fifteenth, Twenty-second, and Twenty-third Divisions. According to the three-three system, each battalion consisted of three infantry companies. The battalion headquarters had a heavy machine gun platoon, equipped with two heavy machine guns. Most of the soldiers were new recruits, with very few veterans. There was an extreme shortage of cadres. In each battle, cadre casualties accounted for half of the soldiers. The organization of the entire bandit army, with the First, Second, and Fifteenth Divisions belonging to the First Army Corps, led by Corps Commander Lin Biao, Political Commissar Nie Yunzhen, Chief of Staff Zuo Quan, and Director of the Political Department Li Zhuoran. The Fourth, Fifth, and Sixth Divisions belonged to the Third Army Corps, led by Corps Commander Peng Dehuai, Political Commissar Yang Shangkun, Chief of Staff Bu Ping, and Director of the Political Department Yuan Guoping. The Thirteenth and Fourteenth Divisions belonged to the Fifth Army Corps, led by Corps Commander Dong Zhentang (formerly the brigade commander of Sun Lianzhong's division who defected to the bandit army in 1931), Political Commissar Zhu Duan, and Director of the Political Department Liu Baijian. The Chief of Staff was vacant. The Red bandit pseudo-Military Commission designated the First, Third, and Fifth Army Corps as assault brigades, gathering them for decisive battles. The Seventh Army Corps had the Fifteenth Division, with Corps Commander and Division Commander Xun Huaizhou, Political Commissar Le Shaohua, Chief of Staff Li Yu, and Director of the Political Department Liu Ying. This army corps had approximately 4,300 soldiers and 1,700 guns, responsible for containing the enemy on the eastern side of the bandit area. The Ninth Army Corps was led by Commander and Division Commander Luo Binghui, Political Commissar Cai Shufan, and the Chief of Staff was vacant. This army corps had approximately 3,600 soldiers and 2,000 guns, responsible for containing the enemy on the northeastern side of the bandit area. After July, the main forces of the army corps acted strangely.

Statistically, the entire bandit army was divided into fourteen divisions, three supplementary divisions, six independent regiments, and two training regiments, totaling 86,700 people with 33,800 guns (number, personnel, and name of the chief omitted). However, due to the battles of August and September, more than 10,000 people abandoned their weapons and fled home. The locations of the pseudo-military districts, leaders, and their subordinate soldiers are listed as follows: 1. Jiangxi Military District, Commander Chen Yi, with one division and three independent regiments, stationed in Luokou (under Ningdu), responsible for defending the northwest lines of the bandit area; 2. Fujian Military District, Ye Jianying, with a central division stationed in Tingzhou, responsible for defending the eastern lines of the bandit area; 3. (Min-Gan Military District Shao Shiping), with one regiment and small guerrilla units, originally stationed in Anyuan Ninghua, responsible for defending the northeast lines of the bandit area; 4. Guangdong-Jiangxi Military District, Commander He Changgong, with one division and an independent regiment stationed in Huichang, responsible for defending the southern lines of the bandit area; 5. Southern Jiangxi Military District, Commander Xiang Ying, with two regiments stationed in Yudu, responsible for defending the southwest lines of the bandit area. The organization of the Red bandit pseudo-Central Military Commission is the highest military command agency of the bandit army, modeled after the Red Army organization of the Red Machine. It is divided into six departments: 1. General Headquarters (i.e., General Staff Department); 2. General Political Department; 3. General Supply Department (i.e., Quartermaster Department); 4. General Health Department (i.e., Military Medical Department); 5. General Logistics Department; 6. General Mobilization and Armaments Department (managing the bandit army's troop strength, replenishment, and independent small units). In addition to the six departments, there is also a Secretariat and a pseudo-Chemical Research Laboratory (responsible for air defense and poison gas). Each army corps and military district also has four departments: Command, Political, Supply, and Health (the military district also has a Mobilization and Armaments Department). Bandit leader Zhu De is the Chairman of the pseudo-Central Military Commission, Zhou Enlai and Wang Jiaxiang are the Vice Chairmen, Li De (a Russian who entered the bandit area in August of last year) is the advisor, Liu Bocheng is the Chief of General Staff, Wang Jiaxiang is also the Director of the Political Department, He Chang is the Deputy Director, Ye Lizhuang is the Minister of Supply, He Cheng is the Minister of Health, Yang Lisan is the Director of the General Logistics Department, and Knee Daiyuan is the Director of the General Mobilization and Armaments Department.

The following factories are under the pseudo-Military Commission: (A) Ordnance Factory, located near Ruijin Ruilinjia, with more than 100 workers, manufacturing explosives and bullets, and domestically-made rifles; (B) Radio and Communications Equipment Factory, with only eleven shortwave radios, two for each of the three army corps, one each for the 5th, 7th, and 9th Armies, and one each for the Jiangxi and Fujian-Jiangxi Military Districts, and one for the pseudo-Military Commission. There is also a longwave radio, used to communicate with Vladivostok; (C) Communications Materials Factory, located seven miles east of Ruijin, lacking gasoline and kerosene. Only the supplies seized in Zhangzhou the previous year remain, enough for three or four months. Radio materials are also extremely scarce; (D) Pseudo-Health Department, managing eleven rear hospitals and two disability homes. Usually, there are 1,500 to 2,000 wounded and sick officers and soldiers, and more than 10,000 disabled. In total, there are 20 to 30 bandit army hospitals, with a constant population of over 20,000 wounded and sick soldiers. Medicines are extremely scarce. The health materials factory only produces Chinese medicine decoctions to replace Western medicine. Gauze is replaced with thin cotton cloth, and cotton is generally ripped from old cotton clothes. The wounded and sick soldiers are in unbearable conditions. There are frequent suicides in the hospitals. Therefore, junior officers and soldiers of the bandit army generally say that they would rather be killed than be sent to the rear. As for the bandit army's supplies and the morale of junior and middle-ranking officers and soldiers, before July of last year, the bandit army's meals cost 1.5 jiao (paper yuan) per person per day. From January to March/April of this year, the cost of meals was reduced to 1.2 jiao per person. After the Central Army captured Guangchang and Jianning, the bandit army uniformly issued grain. During marches, each person received 1.4 jin of rice per day and 4 fen for vegetables. When stationed, each person received 1 jin of rice per day (two meals a day). No money has been issued for two years. Straw sandals are made by the soldiers themselves. Because the National Army blocked the bandit area, no cloth or cotton was allowed into the area. Last winter, cotton clothes were only issued to two-thirds of the soldiers, and a large part of them were old cotton clothes that had been worn for several years and were tattered. No summer uniforms were issued this spring, and for the autumn cotton clothes, the bandit leaders ordered the soldiers' families to send them to the army. Salt is extremely scarce in the bandit area. Each paper yuan can only buy eight qian of salt. Since the bandit army withdrew from Guangchang, Jianning, Liancheng, Yunmenling, etc., they have been constantly eating bland food. The lives of the Red bandit officers and soldiers are extremely miserable. They generally have two kinds of mentality: those who live outside the bandit area constantly think of defecting, while those who live in the bandit area often plan to abandon their weapons and return home. However, the Red Party and bandit leaders Zhu De, Mao Zedong, etc., knowing that the military's morale is wavering, closely monitor the junior and middle-ranking officers and soldiers in the bandit army in order to prolong their lives. Each level of officers is assigned a political commissar to monitor them. All orders and notifications are not effective unless signed by the Political Committee. Military officers have command authority but no administrative authority. They also set up a security bureau and special commissioners to deploy many secret detectives (the so-called political detective network). Therefore, soldiers who are slightly careless in their words or whose attitudes change are immediately arrested. Currently, bandit leaders prohibit three to five people from gathering and talking in the bandit army.

The pseudo-Central government has established the following military schools: (A) Red Army University, located at Dashuxia in the lower Xiao District, ten miles from Ruijin. The principal is Zhou Kun, who once served as the commander of the pseudo-Fourth Army. His left leg is disabled. There are approximately 200-300 students, divided into a senior class, an advanced command course, and an advanced staff course, training cadres above the battalion and regimental level; (B) Peng Yang Infantry School, located in Jiubao, Ruijin. The principal is Chen Yu. There are 1,000 students who will graduate in April, also training company and platoon cadres; (C) Gonglue Infantry School, located near Yudu City. The principal is Lin Ye. There are 800-900 students who will graduate in April, also training company and platoon cadres; (D) Special Forces School, located in Ruijin Wuchangtuan. The principal is Hu Guojie. There are 400-500 students, divided into artillery, engineering, heavy machine gun teams, and anti-aircraft gun teams. They graduate in one year; (E) Local Cadre School, located in Shangxiafang near Ruijin. The principal is Liu Yunhai. There are over 300 students, who are cadres sent from various guerrilla teams, independent regiments, and Red Garrison Armies. They graduate in three months; (F) Radio School, the principal is Mr. Liu, with 100 students. They graduate in one and a half years; (G) Health School, the principal is Chen Yihou. Except for the Radio and Health Schools, the rest are armed, equipped with various weapons, ready for battle. This is also the pseudo-Central government's garrison force. (October 26th)

Fujian Province Raises Funds for Disaster Relief 90

The Fujian Province Fundraising Team is Established

Chen Yi Serves as the Chief Captain

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian authorities previously stated that the province had suffered from banditry and drought for years, and that the disaster areas were vast and the disaster situation was severe, urgently requiring relief. They specially dispatched Li Guodian, the third section chief of the Department of Civil Affairs, to Nanjing and Nanchang to request relief. He returned to Fujian the day before yesterday. According to his report, he was ordered to report the disaster situation in the province to the Relief Committee in Beijing and request relief. The committee stated that it was experiencing financial difficulties and agreed to do its best to request funds from the Ministry of Finance, but the Ministry of Finance stated that the national treasury was stretched and could only help find a way, so it was difficult to predict when the funds could be remitted to Fujian. He then went to Jiangxi to report to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek on the situation. Secretary-General Yang appeared on Chiang's behalf and also said that the expeditionary headquarters was experiencing financial difficulties and was unable to provide relief to the disaster-stricken provinces, ordering them to devise their own proper solutions. Therefore, this trip yielded no results. Since the central government was unable to help, the provincial government decided to organize a fundraising team to appeal to philanthropists at home and abroad, to gather contributions and provide relief to the disaster victims. Chairman Chen Yi himself served as the Chief Captain of the Fujian Province Fundraising Team. The provincial government sent letters to the department heads of the province, the administrative inspectors of each district, the chairmen of chambers of commerce in commercial ports, and the chairmen of Fujian associations in various provinces, and the chairmen of Fujian guilds on the islands of Southeast Asia, appointing more than 50 people as team leaders. The appointment letters and donation books were issued yesterday, hoping that they would follow the procedures, establish fundraising teams, and immediately embark on fundraising. The deadline for establishment is the middle of November at the latest, and the deadline for completion is the end of March next year, reporting once every month on the 15th to facilitate comparison. Meanwhile, Li Zuyu, the head of the Department of Civil Affairs and the chairman of the Provincial Relief Committee, sent a letter to Xu Shiying, chairman of the National Relief Committee, detailing the disaster situation in the province and requesting relief. The letter stated that since the summer of this year, the weather in Fujian Province has been erratic, starting with continuous rain for many days, causing floods. Twenty-five counties, including Minhou, have suffered from floods. The extent of the disaster and the severity of the situation have been reported and verified. Subsequently, severe droughts occurred, and farmland cracked. The autumn harvest is hopeless. Six counties, including Putian, Pingnan, Yongchun, Fuqing, Yongding, and Minhou, have already reported drought disasters. The disaster and suffering in Fujian Province have reached an extreme point. This year's floods and droughts are even more devastating. How can the people bear it? It is reported that you are holding meetings in Shanghai to raise funds for urgent relief in various provinces. The disaster situation in Fujian Province is severe, no less than other provinces, and should be included in the list of those needing relief. It is hoped that you will quickly distribute large sums of money to relieve the suffering. We will pray without end. In addition, when the Red banditry was rampant last spring and summer, there were as many as 5,000 to 6,000 refugees from northwestern Fujian fleeing to the province. At that time, temples and ancestral halls inside and outside the city were filled. Subsequently, the government, the chamber of commerce, and various charities jointly established a refugee relief office, accommodating the refugees in Huangshan Township in the southern district, distributing food and clothing according to their needs. The treatment was quite considerate. This summer, the counties in the bandit area were successively recovered, and the refugees were sent back to their hometowns in batches. Currently, only 700-800 refugees from Changting, Ninghua, Qingliu, and Mingxi counties remain, still without homes to return to. Now the relief office is running out of funds, and providing supplies is difficult. They plan to allocate the strong laborers as road construction workers to reduce the burden. (October 23rd)

Director Yu's Speech at the Baojia Meeting of Jiangnan Counties 91

To urge all counties under the jurisdiction of Jiangnan and Jiangdu districts to earnestly implement the Baojia system, the Zhenjiang Commissioner's Office and the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Department convened county magistrates from various counties in the province in batches on the 20th and 27th of this month to hold Baojia meetings, instructing them on the procedures and methods of implementation. The following is a transcript of Director Yu's speech to the county magistrates present:

First of all, county magistrates, after hearing your reports today, I know that you have a deep understanding and detailed study of the meaning of Baojia and its laws and regulations. Therefore, I know that you do not treat the orders of the Provincial Department as mere formalities, but are determined to implement them. This is something that I am very pleased about.

The meaning of Baojia is already clear to everyone, so I won't repeat it. I would now like to specifically discuss with you the spirit of the Baojia system, as I perceive it. The Baojia system is a local political system passed down from ancient China. It is a grassroots basic organization of local politics. The characteristic of this organization is that it takes the household as the unit. In other words, it takes the family as the unit, which is clearly different from all organizations in Europe and America that take the individual as the unit. The foundation of this organization is the family, and the foundation of this organization is built on ethical kinship. This is the characteristic of the Baojia system, and it is also its spirit. The requirement of the Baojia system is that each household should have a good head of household. A household is a family, and we hope that each family will have a good head of the family to manage the children of the family and not allow bad people to associate with them. Ten households form a Jia, and the Jia has a Jia head. We hope that there will be a good Jia head or good family head within each Jia or ten households to manage the children of these ten households and not allow bad people to associate with them. Ten Jia form a Bao, and the Bao has a Bao head. We hope that there will be a good Bao head or a good family head within each Bao or hundred households to manage the children of these hundred households and not allow them to associate with bad people. The inherent spirit of the Chinese family is most representative of the spirit of Chinese ethics. Most obvious is that the family is rich in the spirit of eliminating violence and maintaining peace, and rich in the spirit of helping those in need. Unfortunately, if an unruly child appears in the city, the head of the family must use family law to punish him. In places where families live together, the clan head can even use his authority to supervise or punish his unfilial children, and even expel them from the clan. This is the spirit of eliminating violence and maintaining peace. Not only that, but the spirit of the family is also full of the spirit of helping those in need. Poor children and impoverished clan members often rely on it to survive. For example, the charity estates and farm fields that exist in history or everywhere now are concrete manifestations of this spirit. What is regrettable is that China has been influenced by modern trends, and even this spirit within the family has gradually disappeared. Therefore, when we implement Baojia, we want to restore this spirit, promote it, and develop it beyond the family, from the family to the nation that Dr. Sun Yat-sen spoke of, which is the principle of regulating the family and governing the country. I feel that the fundamental spirit of Baojia lies entirely in this.

Baojia is a tool, not an end. This tool is a tool for organizing and training the people. Therefore, if Baojia is done well, it means that the people are well organized. When the people are well organized, we can then train the people. When the people are well trained, we can use them however we want. If we want to use them in a passive way, we can use them for self-defense, eliminating violence and maintaining peace, as village police, as local self-defense troops, or as cells of the national defense army. If we want to use them in an active way, we can build roads, develop water conservancy, train the four powers, and carry out all other social or material construction, becoming the basic team for all self-governance undertakings. In recent years, there have been many bandits in various places, and local security sometimes has problems. In addition, the international situation is dangerous, and local self-defense has become a unanimous requirement. Naturally, there is an urgent need for Baojia. Even in terms of self-governance, Jiangsu has been implementing self-governance for several years, but what are the results? Therefore, in order to strive to complete self-governance, we must also quickly implement Baojia and organize this basic tool of self-governance well. Some people mistakenly believe that Jiangsu is implementing Baojia without implementing self-governance. They do not know that Baojia is a tool and self-governance is the goal. We naturally want to implement Baojia for the sake of local self-defense, so as to achieve the goal of self-defense. We want to implement Baojia even more in order to complete local self-governance in Jiangsu, so as to achieve the goal of self-governance. I often find a very strange and dangerous phenomenon in Chinese society, that is, good people are not organized, and good people who are law-abiding are not organized, while bandits have bandit organizations, hooligans have hooligan organizations, and even beggars have beggar organizations. Organization is a kind of power. If good people are not organized, it means that good people have no power. If bad people are organized, it means that bad people have power. How dangerous is this phenomenon! If this continues, without foreigners coming to destroy China, the good people of China will gradually be eliminated by the bad people of China. The use of Baojia is to organize good people, use the power of good people, eliminate the evils of society, and promote the progress of society. Since Baojia is so important, this province decided to implement Baojia this spring, and set progressive steps. The counties under the jurisdiction of the five administrative inspectorates of Tongshan, Hai'an, Huaiyin, Nantong, and Yancheng in Jiangbei will implement it first, followed by the Jiangdu District and the various Jiangnan districts, stipulating that implementation should begin in April. Later, due to various reasons, the progress was slightly delayed (to be continued)

Songjiang 93

Tragic Incident of Severed Ankle While Watching a Movie

The Boy Scouts of the Second District of our province recently gathered at the local primary school in this county to hold a grand review and camp. The event lasted for three days. Residents of Songjiang flocked to see it, creating a rare grand occasion. Yesterday was the second day of the event. Starting at 7 pm, a movie was shown, attracting many viewers. An elderly woman, Zhang Zhao, who lived in front of the Mo Mansion and made a living as a domestic helper, had never been to a movie theater in her life, due to her lifelong hard work. Taking advantage of this free viewing opportunity, she was invited by a neighbor to go along. Reaching the primary school, just as the movie was being shown, the ground was pitch black. She accidentally stepped into a hole with her right foot, fell to the ground, and was in excruciating pain. The Boy Scouts present, upholding the spirit of rescue, hired a car to take her to Songjiang Hospital for treatment. It was discovered that her right ankle bone was broken. In order to save her life, it was necessary to amputate her right foot in order to have hope of survival. However, the old woman was alone and made a living as a domestic helper. The amputation has not yet been resolved, and her poverty and illness are pitiful.

Conclusion of the Extortion Case Debate 94

Wang Baoyuan, a resident of Xita Alley with modest assets, received a threatening letter at the beginning of the month under the name of the "Jiangzhe Iron-Blooded Army." The letter demanded three hundred yuan, instructing Wang to negotiate at the Release Pond, otherwise the whole family's lives would be sacrificed. The case was reported to the Second Police Station. Patrol Officer Lang Xianong, together with the Detective Team Leader, went to the Release Pond, and arrested Yu Yaozhang and Lu Jiuxian, who looked suspicious. A fake gun was found on Lu. They were both sent to the Public Security Bureau and then to the court for investigation. As reported previously, after Yu was arrested, an envelope printed with the words "Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party" was found in his home, matching the threatening letter. After comparing the handwriting, Yu finally confessed and repeatedly claimed that he had been fooled. Today, the prosecutor filed a public prosecution, and Judge Zhang Yihuang of the Criminal Court summoned the case for trial. First, Patrol Officer Lang Xianong of the Second Police Station testified about the arrest. Yu Yaozhang then admitted his guilt without denial, but Lu Jiuxian firmly denied it, and defense lawyer Zhang Bingyuan made a defense. The judge announced the conclusion of the debate and scheduled sentencing for the 31st. According to reports, Yu and Lu are both 21 years old and still young. Lu was studying in Shanghai. Lawyer Zhang's request for bail was not granted, and they were both detained.

Taicang 95

Patrol Officer Sentenced to Imprisonment for Malfeasance

Chen Hezhen, the daughter of Chen Qinren, the owner of the Chen Fuji store in Zhitang, had an affair with her cousin and absconded to Suzhou with clothes and jewelry. Chen Qinren later found her and handed over both the person and the stolen goods to the Fifth Police Station of this county, requesting legal action. After persuasion from relatives of both families, they reconciled. Zhou Jingming, the patrol officer of the police station, extorted two hundred yuan in bribes, but failed. He then hid a portion of the seized gold jewelry, totaling eight items such as gold hairpins and pearl flowers, and did not hand them over. Chen reported the matter to the county government. After several trials, the sentence has been pronounced, sentencing Zhou Jingming to eight months of imprisonment, suspended for three years, and requiring a cash guarantee of six hundred yuan. Two reputable shops in the city will serve as guarantors. Before guarantors are found, he will remain in the custody of the County Public Security Bureau.

Suzhou 96

Reactions to the National Goods Exhibition

Recently, merchants such as Sun Zicheng have organized a mobile national goods exhibition to promote national goods. They have borrowed the vacant land of the YMCA and built sheds as exhibition venues, inviting various manufacturers to participate in the mobile exhibition, charging each company a rent of thirty yuan, with electricity and advertising costs excluded. They have submitted the plan to the County Party Department for the record, and have hired Cheng Ganqing, a standing committee member of the County Chamber of Commerce, as the chairman, and Xue Yongling, chairman of the Shanghai Foreign Goods Association, as the vice chairman. The opening is scheduled for November 10th. When the members of the Shanghai Foreign Goods Association and the Hangzhou Silk Goods Association heard this news, they believed that Sun and others were using the promotion of national goods as a guise to reap profits and that it would greatly affect the business of various department stores, so they were greatly alarmed. On the evening of the 28th, the members went to Cheng Ganqing's residence to demand justice. Mr. Cheng replied that the goods in the stores were mostly from national goods factories in Shanghai, without distinction, so he had declined the position of chairman. The members then dispersed.

Farmers in Huqiu Petition for Disaster Investigation 97

Farmers in the Huqiu Eighteen Tu area outside the Chang Gate, because the county government had not sent anyone to investigate the disaster situation in the area, yesterday (29th), dozens of male and female farmers, each holding dead rice seedlings, petitioned the county government, requesting a disaster investigation. County Magistrate Wu agreed to send someone to investigate immediately, and the farmers were satisfied and returned.

Infatuated with Prostitutes, He Enters Prison 98

Since the case of Chen Ming, an employee of the Shanghai Bank, embezzling a large sum of money occurred, the detective team here has been paying close attention to suspicious travelers from other places. Gu Wenzao, who lives at No. 12 Jin Si Lane, Huishan Road, Shanghai, used to be a stock exchange worker and is a dissolute young man. He came to Suzhou a few days ago and stayed at No. 48 Sanxin Hotel on Dama Road. He met a prostitute named Wang Xuefang. The two fell in love at first sight and regretted not having met sooner. They had been living together for several nights. Gu spent money like dirt, which was discovered by the detective team, which feared that it was related to the Chen case. They immediately sent detectives to arrest the man and woman and found a deposit book of the Shanghai Pudong Bank for 1,200 yuan. They have been sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Wuxi

Slaughter Tax Causes Another Dispute 99

The local slaughter tax in this county has been implemented by the tax office since the 16th of this month, collecting taxes at a slightly higher rate. However, pork from rural areas is not allowed to be brought into the urban area, causing opposition from the restaurant and noodle shop industries, who believe that the meat from rural areas has already been taxed for slaughter, but is not allowed to be brought in, and the tax office is deliberately making things difficult, disturbing the market. According to past practice, meat brought from rural areas for personal use within 20 jin was not subject to inspection. Yesterday, a letter was sent to the County Chamber of Commerce, requesting it to forward a letter to the County Government, requesting it to order the Slaughter Tax Collection Office to pay special attention, and to allow the free use of meat purchased from rural areas if the invoice and weight match, and not to arbitrarily harass them, so as to stabilize business and prevent disputes.

Strictly Arrest the Murder Suspect 100

Wang Jinsheng and Wang Quanbao, brothers who are fishermen living in a boat under the shed outside the West Gate, were selling fish at the Tianhou Temple field under the bridge a few days ago. They fought over customers. Quanbao was kicked in the lower abdomen by Quansheng, and died from his injuries. Afterwards, Chen Zizhao, the leader of the Twenty-Seventh Tu, together with the deceased's wife, Wang Fang, reported the case to the local branch court. Prosecutor Shen went to examine the body and determined that he died from the injuries. He ordered Fang to put the body in a coffin and wait for the arrest of the murderer to be dealt with according to law. It is now learned that the principal murderer, Wang Quansheng, has secretly returned to Wuxi, trying to escape the law. After receiving the report, the Procuratorate of the local branch court has sent police to strictly arrest him in order to deal with him according to law.

The Xiaohuo Public Security Branch Arrests Bandits 101

Zhou Daonan, a patrol officer of the Third Police Station directly under the Xiaohuo Town Public Security Bureau in Wuyi, recently received a tip-off that Zhang Lianpeng, a wanted criminal in the Xia Zi Zhou robbery case, was hiding in his home. At about 8 pm on the 27th, he led several policemen to the address to arrest him. The bandit Zhang Guilin was wearing a Zhongshan suit and riding breeches. Seeing the police, he knew that things were not going well, and immediately inserted his hand into his breeches pocket, intending to take out a gun and shoot. The police rushed forward and tied both of his hands. A White Langlin pistol was found in his pocket, with two bullets loaded. Several stolen goods were also found. At the same time, two bandits, Chen Longying and Zhu Danyun, were arrested nearby and taken to the police station. After preliminary interrogation by the patrol officer, Zhu Danyun confessed to committing many crimes, while the other two criminals remained silent. On the 29th, he prepared a document and sent police to escort them to the county government for interrogation.

Letter

Letter from Changshu Electric Factory 114

To the Editor of the Shanghai Shen Bao,

I have read the Changshu communication on page three of your newspaper on October 25th, regarding the electrical dispute which has been satisfactorily resolved. This is not in accordance with the facts. Our factory handles business and has established operating regulations approved by the Construction Committee for implementation. We operate in accordance with the regulations everywhere and there is absolutely no violation. Now reading the communication, it says that our factory has taken back the fire meter and changed it to a rental system, and abolished the comparator fee, etc., which are all based on unfounded rumours. As for the fact that Mr. Guo Zhicheng, Chairman of the Suzhou Electric Association, invited user representatives to talk on the 23rd, it was to explain misunderstandings. After the talk, the association sent a letter to the user representatives, declaring everything, and there were no decision-making methods. For this reason, I am writing to request a correction, and I hope that it will be published in the letter column. I would like to offer my best wishes. Sincerely, Changshu Electric Factory Co., Ltd. 23.10.2

The Eurasia Company's Lanzhou-Baotou Route Opens Regularly 115

Today, a plane will be sent from Shanghai to Lanzhou for the first flight.

Packages and mail can arrive within two days.

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, the Eurasia Aviation Company is developing air traffic in the Northwest and has expanded the Shanghai-Xinjiang route, preparing to add a branch line from Lanzhou to Baotou. After Meng Tifu, the director of the flight group, went to Baotou from Shanghai last week to tidy up the airport and station buildings, he telegraphed Shanghai to report that everything was ready. It is now learned that the company has decided to send a plane from Shanghai to Lanzhou today (i.e., the scheduled flight of the Shanghai-Xinjiang route), and then officially open the flight from Lanzhou to Baotou on the first of next month. The line is connected to the stations of the PingSui Railway, which is very convenient for passengers and mail. The postal administration has formulated methods for receiving and sending mail from Shanghai to Baotou. Various mails sent from Shanghai can arrive in Baotou within two days.

The Post Office Announces the Resumption of Regular Flights Between Shanghai and Guangzhou 116

Can Arrive on the Same Day

Shanghai Postal Administration Notice No. 1174: The China Aviation Company's Shanghai-Guangzhou route was temporarily suspended from April 16th of this year, as announced in Notice No. 1135. Now, according to a letter from the China Aviation Company, the Shanghai-Guangzhou route will be scheduled to fly from Shanghai to Guangzhou every Friday from November 2nd, and from Guangzhou back to Shanghai every Sunday. The time of departure is 6:30 am, and it will arrive on the same day. However, from December 1st, it will be changed to two round trips per week, i.e., Shanghai to Guangzhou on Tuesdays and Fridays, and Guangzhou to Shanghai on Thursdays and Sundays. Hereby announced for general knowledge.

New Stamp Tax Sold Ahead of Schedule Today 117

Old Stamps Allowed to be Exchanged Within the Year

Central News Agency: The Ministry of Finance has announced the new stamp tax law, which will be implemented on the first of next month. New stamps will be sold starting today to facilitate merchants' purchase and affixing. As for the method of exchanging old stamps, it has not yet been decided. According to reporters, the situation is as follows:

Differences Between New and Old Stamp Tax 118

The Ministry of Finance has announced the new stamp tax law and issued new stamps, which will be implemented on the first of next month. The new tax law differs from the current stamp regulations in several points: 1. Certificates of common acts, such as shipping documents, must be affixed starting from three yuan. 2. Receipts for money are tax-free within three yuan, and one cent is still affixed from three yuan to ten yuan. 3. Invoices for goods priced at more than ten yuan adopt a progressive tax system, with an increase of one cent for every ten yuan, up to a limit of one yuan. 4. Invoices for money increase by one cent for every ten yuan or more.

New Stamps Begin to be Sold Today 119

The new stamp tax is scheduled to be affixed from the first of next month and will be sold by post offices and postal and telecommunications offices in various places. Tobacco and exchange shops will not be sold. In order to avoid crowding by merchants, the Tax Administration has notified the post offices in this port to start selling them early this morning. However, other ports will still be sold from the first of the month.

Old Stamps Temporarily Not Allowed to be Affixed 120

Regarding the matter of old stamps being invalidated and not allowed to be used again, after strong efforts by various merchants, the Ministry of Finance has agreed to allow them to be exchanged for new stamps within this year. The Minister has telegraphed Fang Huixian, the chief of the stamp, alcohol and tobacco tax section of the Tax Administration, to go to Beijing to discuss the method. Director Fang has now returned to Shanghai after completing his official duties, but the method has not yet been decided and is expected to be announced at the beginning of next month. Before the method is announced, old stamps are temporarily not allowed to be affixed.

He Yingqin Visits National Goods Factory 121

Commends the China Stone Company

The Minister of Military Administration, He Yingqin, heard that the China Stone Company is a purely domestic stone company, and that the projects it has sent to various places have achieved obvious results and are well-known at home and abroad. Therefore, yesterday, together with Li Dachao, section chief of the municipal government, he drove to the Bazihua Bridge in Zhabei to visit the Shanghai branch of the company. Yao Huasun, the general manager of the company, and Wu Nankai, the factory director, accompanied him to visit various departments, such as sawing, grinding, and refrigeration. He inquired in detail about all aspects of the machines, carving, and manual labor. General Manager Yao explained everything in detail, and he was impressed by the various colors of stone blocks and slabs, which were colorful and stood in various fields, and the beautiful products made could also be ingenious. He nodded frequently and expressed deep appreciation, saying that since domestic products are available, why seek them abroad? He hoped that it would be widely promoted so that the Chinese people would know where to use them, and the future would be very bright. The Minister was in high spirits and very interested that day. He learned that the company not only used completely domestic stone materials, but also all the machinery and labor were created and managed by Chinese people. In the future, it will enrich the country and benefit the people, and consider both. After admiring it, he asked for a pen and wrote "Enrich the Country and Benefit the People" to praise it and encourage it.

Praise for the America-Asia Silk Weaving Factory 122

Minister of Military Administration He Yingqin has been in Shanghai on official business for many days. He has always paid attention to industrial production, and he has spared no effort in encouraging the domestic goods production industry. He has been extremely busy visiting domestic goods factories for several days. Yesterday afternoon, accompanied by Li Dachao, the chief of the First Section of the Municipal Government, he visited the America-Asia Silk Weaving Factory. He was personally received by Cai Shengbai, the general manager of the factory. Mr. He greatly praised the factory and wrote the nine characters "Chinese people should use Chinese goods." According to what he told reporters, in promoting domestic goods clothing, in addition to cloth, silk should also be actively promoted. China is a silk-producing country, and in the provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, hundreds of thousands of people rely on silk for a living. If it is not used freely in the country, it will have a real impact on the livelihoods of farmers. The influx of foreign silk into North China is especially something that factories like the America-Asia Silk Factory should use to promote domestic silk in large quantities to recover lost profits.

Guo Dixian from the Zhejiang Department of Finance Supervises

The Silver Export Equalization Tax Is Paid on the Day of Customs Declaration 126

According to the National News Agency in this city, it was recently announced by the spokesman of the Central Bank that, according to reliable sources, the suggestion of Minister of Finance Kong for the Foreign Exchange Market Equalization Committee has been ordered to the Customs to allow those who transport silver for export to pay the equalization tax to be levied on the day of customs declaration (that is, those who transport silver for export can avoid the difficulty of not being able to predict the amount of tax to be paid). According to this method, one can prove the government's sole will to prevent silver from being transported for export due to speculation, and two can prove that the government still maintains its silver standard system for the Chinese monetary system, and three can allow banks to offset their positions when necessary in foreign exchange. According to the spokesman, Minister of Finance Kong also instructed the Customs to not levy additional taxes and dredging fees on the tax when collecting the equalization tax.

The Tongde Wheel Ran Aground in Tongzhou 128

The Ningjing Also Ran Aground in Shashi

The Tongde Wheel of the Tongde Company is managed by the Dafang Company on Hankou Road in this city. On the 27th of this month, it loaded 3,800 shuns of Fuyuan coal from the Tongzhangpu area downstream of Hankou and came to Shanghai. The journey was safe. When the ship arrived in Tongzhou on the night of the 28th, there was fog in Jiangxi. Due to careless leading of the river, the ship entered a shallow sandbank and ran aground. Although the shipowner tried every means to reverse the engine to escape, the water on the beach was too shallow, and the Tongde Wheel could not drive out because it was heavily loaded. Yesterday, a telegram was sent to Shanghai to report the incident and request rescue. The company has consulted with the British Taikoo Company and requested that the Huangpu Wheel, which left Shanghai upstream on the 27th, should help tow the ship when it arrives in Tongzhou. Taikoo has agreed and has sent a telegram to the owner of the Huangpu ship to help rescue it.

In addition, the Yongsheng and Yunlong salt transport ships that ran aground in Shashi have sent telegrams saying that the Yongsheng Wheel has cleared the salt and been rescued from the shoal, and will be repaired in Shanghai immediately. The Yunlong Wheel is still stranded on the shoal in Shashi. The Ningshao Company's Ningjing Wheel also transported salt from Haizhou to Sha this time. Because the ship was large and the water was shallow, it also ran aground. The two ships are unloading the salt in the ship before being towed.
